<s> on the table are an open bottle of claret his hat and some tea things <\s>
<s> down in the hearth is a kettle on a lighted spirit stand <\s>
<s> near the door stands haywood a short round faced man with a tobacco coloured moustache malise by the table is contemplating a piece of blue paper <\s>
<s> sorry to press an old customer sir but a year and an alf without any return on your money malise <\s>
<s> your tobacco is too good mr <\s>
<s> i wish i could see my way to smoking another <\s>
<s> well sir that's a funny remedy <\s>
<s> with a knock on the half opened door a boy appears <\s>
<s> your copy for the watchfire please sir <\s>
<s> motioning him out yes <\s>
<s> malise goes up to the pile of books turns them over and takes up some volumes <\s>
<s> this is a very fine unexpurgated translation of boccaccio's decameron mr <\s>
<s> i should say you would get more than the amount of your bill for them <\s>
<s> shaking his head them books worth three pound seven <\s>
<s> it's scarce and highly improper <\s>
<s> will you take them in discharge <\s>
<s> torn between emotions well i ardly know what to say no sir i don't think i'd like to ave to do with that <\s>
<s> you could read them first you know <\s>
<s> dubiously i've got my wife at ome <\s>
<s> you could both read them <\s>
<s> brought to his bearings no sir i couldn't <\s>
<s> very well i'll sell them myself and you shall have the result <\s>
<s> well thank you sir <\s>
<s> i'm sure i didn't want to trouble you <\s>
<s> not at all mr <\s>
<s> it's for me to apologize <\s>
<s> so long as i give satisfaction <\s>
<s> holding the door for him certainly <\s>
<s> good evenin sir no offence i hope <\s>
<s> and malise stands scratching his head then slipping the bill into one of the volumes to remind him he replaces them at the top of the pile <\s>
<s> the boy again advances into the doorway <\s>
<s> yes now for you <\s>
<s> he goes to the table and takes some sheets of ms <\s>
<s> from an old portfolio <\s>
<s> but the door is again timidly pushed open and haywood reappears <\s>
<s> about that little matter sir <\s>
<s> if if it's any convenience to you i've thought of a place where i could malise <\s>
<s> you'll enjoy them thoroughly <\s>
<s> where i can dispose of them <\s>
<s> holding out the volumes it might be as well <\s>
<s> haywood takes the books gingerly i congratulate you mr <\s>
<s> haywood it's a classic <\s>
<s> in the event of there being any malise <\s>
<s> carry it to my credit <\s>
<s> your bill he hands over the blue paper send me the receipt <\s>
<s> haywood nonplussed and trying to hide the books in an evening paper fumbles out <\s>
<s> malise again takes up the sheets of ms <\s>
<s> and cons a sentence over to himself gazing blankly at the stolid boy <\s>
<s> man of the world good form your god <\s>
<s> poor buttoned up philosopher the boy shifts his feet inbred to the point of cretinism and founded to the bone on fear of ridicule the boy breathes heavily you are the slave of facts <\s>
<s> there is a knock on the door malise <\s>
<s> the door is pushed open and reginald huntingdon stands there <\s>
<s> i apologize sir can i come in a minute <\s>
<s> malise bows with ironical hostility huntingdon <\s>
<s> i don't know if you remember me clare dedmond's brother <\s>
<s> he motions to the stolid boy to go outside again huntingdon <\s>
<s> i've come to you sir as a gentleman malise <\s>
<s> there is one i believe on the first floor <\s>
<s> it's about my sister <\s>
<s> don't you know that i've been shadowed these last three months <\s>
<s> ask your detectives for any information you want <\s>
<s> we know that you haven't seen her or even known where she is <\s>
<s> you've found that out <\s>
<s> we know it from my sister <\s>
<s> so you've tracked her down <\s>
<s> fullarton came across her yesterday in one of those big shops selling gloves <\s>
<s> fullarton the lady with the husband <\s>
<s> clap her back into prison <\s>
<s> we have not got her <\s>
<s> she left at once and we don't know where she's gone <\s>
<s> taking hold of his bit look here mr <\s>
<s> malise in a way i share your feeling but i'm fond of my sister and it's damnable to have to go back to india knowing she must be all adrift without protection going through god knows what <\s>
<s> fullarton says she's looking awfully pale and down <\s>
<s> struggling between resentment and sympathy why do you come to me <\s>
<s> my my father and myself <\s>
<s> we thought there was just a chance that having lost that job she might come to you again for advice <\s>
<s> if she does it would be really generous of you if you'd put my father in touch with her <\s>
<s> he's getting old and he feels this very much <\s>
<s> he hands malise a card this is his address <\s>
<s> twisting the card let there be no mistake sir i do nothing that will help give her back to her husband <\s>
<s> she's out to save her soul alive and i don't join the hue and cry that's after her <\s>
<s> on the contrary if i had the power <\s>
<s> if your father wants to shelter her that's another matter <\s>
<s> but she'd her own ideas about that <\s>
<s> even those who love you <\s>
<s> will they let you be <\s>
<s> the hunt was joined the moment you broke away <\s>
<s> it will never let up <\s>
<s> covert to covert till they've run you down and you're back in the cart and god pity you <\s>
<s> well i'll die running <\s>
<s> let me shelter you <\s>
<s> shaking her head and smiling i'm going to seek my fortune <\s>
<s> i can't let you go <\s>
<s> he looks into her face then realizing that she means it suddenly bends down to her fingers and puts his lips to them <\s>
<s> he releases her hand <\s>
<s> just touching his bent head with her other hand clare turns and goes <\s>
<s> malise remains with bowed head listening to the sound of her receding footsteps <\s>
<s> he raises himself and strikes out into the air with his clenched fist <\s>
